app.use('/',planetroutes)





const express = require('express');
const mongoose = require('mongoose');
const PlanetsInNakshatra = require('./models/plantesInNakshatra'); // Import the model

const router = express.Router();

// Endpoint for bulk update of planets in nakshatras
router.post('/planets-in-nakshatra', async (req, res) => {
    try {
        const updates = req.body; // Expecting an array of objects

        if (!Array.isArray(updates) || updates.length === 0) {
            return res.status(400).json({ message: 'Invalid request format. Expecting an array of updates.' });
        }

        // Fetch the existing document or create a new one if it doesn't exist
        let existingData = await PlanetsInNakshatra.findOne();
        if (!existingData) {
            existingData = new PlanetsInNakshatra({});
        }

        // Allowed planets
        const validPlanets = ['sun', 'moon', 'mars', 'mercury', 'jupiter', 'venus', 'saturn', 'rahu', 'ketu'];

        // Valid Nakshatras
        const nakshatraNames = [
            "Ashwini,अश्विनी", "Bharani,भरणी", "Krittika,कृतिका", "Rohini,रोहिणी",
            "Mrigashira,मृगशिरा", "Ardra,अर्द्रा", "Punarvasu,पुनर्वसु", "Pushya,पुष्य",
            "Ashlesha,आश्लेषा", "Magha,मघा", "Purva_Phalguni,पूर्वाफाल्गुनी", "Uttara_Phalguni,उत्तराफाल्गुनी",
            "Hasta,हस्त", "Chitra,चित्रा", "Swati,स्वाती", "Vishakha,विशाखा",
            "Anuradha,अनुराधा", "Jyeshtha,ज्येष्ठा", "Mula,मूल", "Purva_Ashadha,पूर्वाषाढ़ा",
            "Uttara_Ashadha,उत्तराषाढ़ा", "Shravana,श्रवण", "Dhanishta,धनिष्ठा", "Shatabhisha,शतभिषा",
            "Purva_Bhadrapada,पूर्वभाद्रपदा", "Uttara_Bhadrapada,उत्तराभाद्रपद", "Revati,रेवती"
        ];

        // Valid Padas
        const validPadas = ["1", "2", "3", "4"];

        for (const update of updates) {
            const { planet, nakshatra, padas } = update;

            if (!planet || !nakshatra || !padas) {
                return res.status(400).json({ message: 'Missing required fields: planet, nakshatra, or padas' });
            }

            if (!validPlanets.includes(planet.toLowerCase())) {
                return res.status(400).json({ message: `Invalid planet name: ${planet}` });
            }

            if (!nakshatraNames.includes(nakshatra)) {
                return res.status(400).json({ message: `Invalid nakshatra name: ${nakshatra}` });
            }

            for (const key of Object.keys(padas)) {
                if (!validPadas.includes(key)) {
                    return res.status(400).json({ message: `Invalid pada number: ${key}` });
                }
            }

            // Initialize planet if not present
            if (!existingData[planet]) {
                existingData[planet] = {};
            }

            // Update the nakshatra data
            existingData[planet][nakshatra] = padas;
        }

        // Save the updated document
        await existingData.save();

        res.status(200).json({ message: 'Bulk data updated successfully', data: existingData });
    } catch (error) {
        console.error(error);
        res.status(500).json({ message: 'Server error', error: error.message });
    }
});

module.exports = router;
